----------------------------- MODULE VoteProof_Liveness ------------------------------ 
(***************************************************************************)
(* This is a high-level consensus algorithm in which a set of processes    *)
(* called `acceptors' cooperatively choose a value.  The algorithm uses    *)
(* numbered ballots, where a ballot is a round of voting.  Acceptors cast  *)
(* votes in ballots, casting at most one vote per ballot.  A value is      *)
(* chosen when a large enough set of acceptors, called a `quorum', have    *)
(* all voted for the same value in the same ballot.                        *)
(*                                                                         *)
(* Ballots are not executed in order.  Different acceptors may be          *)
(* concurrently performing actions for different ballots.                  *)
(***************************************************************************)
EXTENDS Integers , FiniteSets, TLC, TLAPS

\* THEOREM SMT == TRUE (*{ by (smt) }*)
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

         Acceptor,  \* The set of all acceptors.
         Quorum     \* The set of all quorums.
 
(***************************************************************************)

  (* that an entire execution of the body of the `while' loop is performed *)
  (* as a single atomic action.                                            *)
  (*                                                                       *)
  (* From this intuitive description of the process declaration, one might *)
  (* think that a process could be deadlocked by choosing a ballot b in    *)
  (* which neither an IncreaseMaxBal(b) action nor any VoteFor(b, v)       *)
  (* action is enabled.  An examination of the TLA+ translation (and an    *)
  (* elementary knowledge of the meaning of existential quantification)    *)
  (* shows that this is not the case.  You can think of all possible       *)
  (* choices of b and of v being examined simultaneously, and one of the   *)
  (* choices for which a step is possible being made.                      *)
  (*************************************************************************)
  process (acceptor \in Acceptor) {
    acc : while (TRUE) {
           with (b \in Ballot) {
             either IncreaseMaxBal(b)
             or     with (v \in Value) { VoteFor(b, v) }
       }
     }
    }
}

(* LiveAssumption.  The WF condition ensures that the acceptors `a' in Q   *)
(* eventually execute the necessary BallotAction(a, b) actions if they are *)
(* enabled, and the [][...]_vars condition ensures that they never perform *)
(* BallotAction actions for higher-numbered ballots, so the necessary      *)
(* BallotAction(a, b) actions are enabled.                                 *)
(***************************************************************************)
LiveAssumption ==
  \E Q \in Quorum, b \in Ballot :
     \A self \in Q :
       /\ WF_vars(BallotAction(self, b))
       /\ [] [\A c \in Ballot : (c > b) => ~ BallotAction(self, c)]_vars
     
LiveSpec == Spec /\ LiveAssumption  
(***************************************************************************)
(* LiveAssumption is stronger than necessary.  Instead of requiring that   *)
(* an acceptor in Q never executes an action of a higher-numbered ballot   *)
(* than b, it suffices that it doesn't execute such an action until unless *)
(* it has voted in ballot b.  However, the natural liveness requirement    *)
(* for a Paxos consensus algorithm implies condition LiveAssumption.       *)
(*                                                                         *)
(* Condition LiveAssumption is a liveness property, constraining only what *)
(* eventually happens.  It is straightforward to replace "eventually       *)
(* happens" by "happens within some length of time" and convert            *)

(* We begin by stating two additional assumptions that are necessary for   *)
(* liveness.  Liveness requires that some value eventually be chosen.      *)
(* This cannot hold with an infinite set of acceptors.  More precisely,    *)
(* liveness requires the existence of a finite quorum.  (Otherwise, it     *)

(***************************************************************************)

(* the requirements are for choosing a value.                              *)

state-change in which the variable `chosen' is changed from its initial
value {} to the value {v} for an arbitrary value v in Value.  The
algorithm itself does not specify any fairness properties, so it also
allows a behavior in which `chosen' is not changed.  We could use a

(***************************************************************************)
(* Here is our proof that LiveSpec implements the specification LiveSpec   *)
(* of module Consensus under our refinement mapping.                       *)
(***************************************************************************)
THEOREM Liveness == LiveSpec => C!LiveSpec
<1> SUFFICES ASSUME NEW Q \in Quorum, NEW b \in Ballot
             PROVE  Spec /\ LiveAssumption!(Q, b) => C!LiveSpec
  BY Isa DEF LiveSpec, LiveAssumption

<1>a. IsFiniteSet(Q)
  BY QA, AcceptorFinite, FS_Subset

<1>1. C!LiveSpec <=> C!Spec /\ ([]<><<C!Next>>_C!vars \/ []<>(chosen # {}))
  BY ValueNonempty, C!LiveSpecEquals

<1> DEFINE LNext == \E self \in Acceptor, c \in Ballot :
                         /\ BallotAction(self, c)
                         /\ (self \in Q) => (c =< b)
                   
<1>2. Spec /\ LiveAssumption!(Q, b) => [][LNext]_vars
  <2>1. /\ TypeOK
        /\ [Next]_vars 
        /\ [\A self \in Q : \A c \in Ballot : (c > b) => ~ BallotAction(self, c)]_vars
        => [LNext]_vars
    BY NextDef DEF LNext, Ballot
  <2>2. /\ []TypeOK 
        /\ [][Next]_vars 
        /\ [][\A self \in Q : \A c \in Ballot : (c > b) => ~ BallotAction(self, c)]_vars
        => [][LNext]_vars
    BY <2>1, PTL
  <2>3. QED
    BY <2>2, VT2, Isa DEF Spec, VInv
  
<1> DEFINE LNInv1 == \A a \in Q : maxBal[a] =< b
           LInv1  == VInv /\ LNInv1
  
... (truncated) ...
  <4> WITNESS votes, [maxBal EXCEPT ![self] = b]
      <4>. QED  BY QA DEF VInv, TypeOK, Ballot
    <3>. QED  BY <3>1, <3>2, <3>3, PTL
  <2>3. QQ /\ [][LNext]_vars => []QQ
    <3>1. QQ /\ [LNext]_vars => QQ'
      BY <1>3, <1>4
    <3>. QED  BY <3>1, PTL
  <2>4. []QQ => [](maxBal[self] = b)
    BY PTL
  <2>5. LiveAssumption!(Q,b) => WF_vars(A)
    BY Isa
  <2>6. Spec => LInv1
    <3>1. Init => VInv
      BY InitImpliesInv
    <3>2. Init => LNInv1
      BY QA DEF Init, Ballot
    <3>. QED  BY <3>1, <3>2 DEF Spec
  <2>. QED
    BY <2>2, <2>3, <2>4, <2>5, <2>6, <1>2, PTL

<1> DEFINE LNInv2 == \A a \in Q : maxBal[a] = b
           LInv2  == VInv /\ LNInv2

<1>7. Spec /\ LiveAssumption!(Q, b) => <>[](chosen # {})
  <2> DEFINE Voted(a) == \E v \in Value : VotedFor(a, b, v)
  <2>1. Spec /\ LiveAssumption!(Q, b) => <>[]LInv2
    <3>1. Spec /\ LiveAssumption!(Q,b) => <>[]LNInv2

      PROOF OMITTED

    <3>1. SUFFICES ASSUME LInv2,
                          \A a \in Q : Voted(a)
                   PROVE  chosen # {}

                          P /\ <<N /\ A>>_f => Q',
                          []P /\ [][N]_f /\ []F => <> ENABLED <<A>>_f
                   PROVE  [][N]_f /\ SF_f(A) /\ []F => (P ~> Q)

(***************************************************************************)
(* The rules WF2 and SF2 in "The Temporal Logic of Actions" are obtained   *)
(* from the following two rules by the following substitutions: `.         *)
(*                                                                         *)
(*          ___        ___         _______________                         *)
(*      M <- M ,   g <- g ,  EM <- ENABLED <<M>>_g       .'                *)
(***************************************************************************)
THEOREM RuleWF2 == ASSUME STATE P, STATE f, STATE g, STATE EM,
                          ACTION A, ACTION B, ACTION N, ACTION M,
                          TEMPORAL F,
                          <<N /\ B>>_f => <<M>>_g,
                          P /\ P' /\ <<N /\ A>>_f /\ EM => B,
                          P /\ EM => ENABLED A,
                          [][N /\ ~B]_f /\ WF_f(A) /\ []F /\ <>[]EM => <>[]P
                   PROVE  [][N]_f /\ WF_f(A) /\ []F => []<><<M>>_g \/ []<>(~EM)

THEOREM RuleSF2 == ASSUME STATE P, STATE f, STATE g, STATE EM,
                          ACTION A, ACTION B, ACTION N, ACTION M,
                          TEMPORAL F,
                          <<N /\ B>>_f => <<M>>_g,
                          P /\ P' /\ <<N /\ A>>_f /\ EM => B,
                          P /\ EM => ENABLED A,

[CMD] /bin/zsh -lc 'head -n 15 /home/ruize/.tlapm15/lib/tlaps/examples/ByzPaxos/VoteProof.tla && rg -n "FS_Subset" ~/.tlapm15/lib/tlaps -S'
----------------------------- MODULE VoteProof ------------------------------ 
(***************************************************************************)
(* This is a high-level consensus algorithm in which a set of processes    *)
(* called `acceptors' cooperatively choose a value.  The algorithm uses    *)
(* numbered ballots, where a ballot is a round of voting.  Acceptors cast  *)
(* votes in ballots, casting at most one vote per ballot.  A value is      *)
(* chosen when a large enough set of acceptors, called a `quorum', have    *)
(* all voted for the same value in the same ballot.                        *)
(*                                                                         *)
(* Ballots are not executed in order.  Different acceptors may be          *)
(* concurrently performing actions for different ballots.                  *)
(***************************************************************************)
EXTENDS Integers, NaturalsInduction, FiniteSets, FiniteSetTheorems, 
        WellFoundedInduction, TLC, TLAPS

[CMD] /bin/zsh -lc "python3 - <<'PY'
from pathlib import Path
p=Path('VoteProof_Liveness.tla')
s=p.read_text()
old='THEOREM Liveness == LiveSpec => C"'!LiveSpec'"\\nPROOF OBVIOUS'
new=r'''THEOREM Liveness == LiveSpec => C"'!LiveSpec
<1> SUFFICES ASSUME NEW Q '"\\in Quorum, NEW b \\in Ballot
             PROVE  Spec /\\ LiveAssumption"'!(Q, b) => C!LiveSpec
  BY Isa DEF LiveSpec, LiveAssumption

<1>a. IsFiniteSet(Q)
  BY QA, AcceptorFinite, SubsetOfFiniteSetFinite

<1>1. C!LiveSpec <=> C!Spec /'"\\ ([]<><<C"'!Next>>_C!vars '"\\/ []<>(chosen # {}))
  BY ValueNonempty, C"'!LiveSpecEquals

<1> DEFINE LNext == '"\\E self \\in Acceptor, c \\in Ballot :
                         /\\ BallotAction(self, c)
                         /\\ (self \\in Q) => (c =< b)
                   
<1>2. Spec /\\ LiveAssumption"'!(Q, b) => [][LNext]_vars
  <2>1. /'"\\ TypeOK
        /\\ [Next]_vars 
        /\\ [\\A self \\in Q : \\A c \\in Ballot : (c > b) => ~ BallotAction(self, c)]_vars
        => [LNext]_vars

  <2>2. /\\ []TypeOK 
        /\\ [][Next]_vars 
        /\\ [][\\A self \\in Q : \\A c \\in Ballot : (c > b) => ~ BallotAction(self, c)]_vars
        => [][LNext]_vars
    BY <2>1, PTL
  <2>3. QED
    BY <2>2, VT2, Isa DEF Spec, VInv
  
<1> DEFINE LNInv1 == \\A a \\in Q : maxBal[a] =< b
           LInv1  == VInv /\\ LNInv1
           
<1>3. LInv1 /\\ [LNext]_vars => LInv1'
  <2>1. SUFFICES ASSUME LInv1, [LNext]_vars 
                 PROVE  LInv1'
    OBVIOUS
  <2>2. VInv'
    BY <2>1, NextDef, InductiveInvariance DEF LInv1, VInv
  <2>3. LNInv1'

  <2>. QED
    BY <2>2, <2>3

otVoteIn(self, b)
                          /\ \A p \in Acceptor \ {self} :
                                \A w \in Value : VotedFor(p, b, w) => (w = v)
                          /\ SafeAt(b, v)
                          /\ votesp = [votes EXCEPT ![self] = votes[self] 
                                                                \cup {<<b, v>>}]
                          /\ maxBalp = [maxBal EXCEPT ![self] = b]
                 /\ <<votesp, maxBalp>> # <<votes, maxBal>>

                             DidNotVoteIn, VotedFor
      <4>. SUFFICES ASSUME P

                              /\ b > maxBal[self]

ControlledEnabled == 
\/ /\ tpos = 0
   /\ tcolor = "black" \/ color[0] = "black"

      /\ tpos = i
      /\ ~ active[i] \/ color[i] = "black" \/ tcolor = "black"

(* If all nodes are inactive, the token must eventually arrive at node 0.  *)
(***************************************************************************)
LEMMA TerminationRound1 ==
  BSpec => (allInactive ~> (allInactive /\ tpos = 0))
<1>. DEFINE P(n) == allInactive /\ n \in Nodes /\ tpos = n
            Q == P(0)
            R(n) == BSpec => [](P(n) => <>Q)
<1>1. \A n \in Nat : R(n)
  <2>1. R(0)
    BY PTL
  <2>2. ASSUME NEW n \in Nat
        PROVE  R(n) => R(n+1)
    <3>. DEFINE Pn == P(n)  Pn1 == P(n+1)
    <3>. USE DEF TypeOK, allInactive, Nodes
    <3>1. TypeOK /\ Pn1 /\ [Next]_vars => Pn1' \/ Pn'
      BY DEF Next, vars, Controlled, Environment, InitiateProbe, PassToken, Deactivate, SendMsg
    <3>2. TypeOK /\ Pn1 /\ <<Controlled>>_vars => Pn'
      BY DEF Controlled, InitiateProbe, PassToken, vars
    <3>3. TypeOK /\ Pn1 => ENABLED <<Controlled>>_vars
      BY EnabledControlled DEF ControlledEnabled
    <3>. HIDE DEF Pn1
    <3>4. R(n) => (BSpec => [](Pn1 => <>Q))
      BY <3>1, <3>2, <3>3, PTL DEF BSpec
    <3>. QED  BY <3>4 DEF Pn1
  <2>. HIDE DEF R
  <2>. QED  \* BY <2>1, <2>2, NatInduction
<1>2. BSpec => []((\E n \in Nat : P(n)) => <>Q)
  <2>. HIDE DEF P, Q
  <2>1. BSpec => [](\A n \in Nat : P(n) => <>Q)

[AGENT] My previous restructuring made the proof shape invalid; I’ll restore the `SUFFICES` shape and give those steps nested proofs.

[AGENT] The proof parses again. I’m waiting for the reduced error list from TLAPS.

[CMD] /bin/zsh -lc "python3 - <<'PY'
from pathlib import Path
p=Path('VoteProof_Liveness.tla')
s=p.read_text()
# Fix first liveness forall block manually via slice replacements
start=s.index('<1>5. Spec /\\\\ LiveAssumption"'!(Q, b) =>'"')
end=s.index('<1> DEFINE LNInv2', start)
block=s[start:end]
block=block.replace('''  <2>1. ASSUME NEW self \\\\in Q
         PROVE  Spec /\\\\ LiveAssumption"'!(Q, b) => <>[](maxBal[self] = b)'"''','''  <2>1. SUFFICES ASSUME NEW self \\\\in Q
                 PROVE  Spec /\\\\ LiveAssumption"'!(Q, b) => <>[](maxBal[self] = b)
    <3>1. ('"\\\\A self \\\\in Q : <>[](maxBal[self] = b))
          => <>[](\\\\A self \\\\in Q : maxBal[self] = b)
      BY <1>a, EventuallyAlwaysForall
    <3>. QED
      BY <3>1, PTL''')
# Remove appended aggregator steps before LNInv2
block=block.replace('''  <2>2. (\\\\A self \\\\in Q : Spec /\\\\ LiveAssumption"'!(Q, b) => <>[](maxBal[self] = b))
        => (Spec /'"\\\\ LiveAssumption"'!(Q, b) => '"\\\\A self \\\\in Q : <>[](maxBal[self] = b))
    BY PTL
  <2>3. (\\\\A self \\\\in Q : <>[](maxBal[self] = b))
        => <>[](\\\\A self \\\\in Q : maxBal[self] = b)
    BY <1>a, EventuallyAlwaysForall
  <2>. QED
    BY <2>1, <2>2, <2>3, PTL

''','')
s=s[:start]+block+s[end:]
# Fix second forall block
start=s.index('  <2>3. Spec /\\\\ LiveAssumption"'!(Q, b) => ('"\\\\A a \\\\in Q : <>[]Voted(a))')
end=s.index('  <2>4. (\\\\A a \\\\in Q : <>[]Voted(a))', start)
block=s[start:end]
block=block.replace('''    <3>1. ASSUME NEW self \\\\in Q
           PROVE  Spec /\\\\ LiveAssumption"'!(Q, b) => <>[]Voted(self)'"''','''    <3>1. SUFFICES ASSUME NEW self \\\\in Q
                   PROVE  Spec /\\\\ LiveAssumption"'!(Q, b) => <>[]Voted(self)
      OBVIOUS'"''')
block=block.replace('''    <3>5. (\\\\A self \\\\in Q : Spec /\\\\ LiveAssumption"'!(Q, b) => <>[]Voted(self))
          => (Spec /'"\\\\ LiveAssumption"'!(Q, b) => '"\\\\A self \\\\in Q : <>[]Voted(self))
      BY PTL
    <3>. QED
      BY <3>1, <3>5, PTL
''','')
s=s[:start]+block+s[end:]
p.write_text(s)
PY

[CMD] /bin/zsh -lc "sed -n '1,260p' check_proof.py"
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Check a single TLAPS benchmark proof for correctness and cheating.

Designed for AI agents to get quick feedback during proof writing.

Usage:
    python3 check_proof.py benchmark/Euclid/GCD_GCD3.tla [--tlapm PATH] [--tlapm-lib PATH] [--timeout SECS]

Output:
    - Raw tlapm output (preserved verbatim)
    - Cheating check (compares against main branch)
    - Summary verdict: PASS / FAIL / CHEATING

Exit codes:
    0 = PASS
    1 = FAIL (proof doesn't verify)
    2 = CHEATING (tampering detected)
    3 = ERROR (could not run check)
"""

import os
import sys
import re
import shutil
import subprocess
import tempfile
import argparse
import glob


def find_tlapm():
    """Find tlapm binary."""
    for candidate in ['/tmp/tlapm15/bin/tlapm', '/tmp/tlapm/bin/tlapm', shutil.which('tlapm')]:
        if candidate and os.path.isfile(candidate):
            return candidate
    return None


def find_tlapm_lib(tlapm_path):
    """Derive lib path from tlapm binary path."""
    base = os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(tlapm_path))
    for sub in ['lib/tlaps', 'lib/tlapm', 'lib']:
        path = os.path.join(base, sub)
        if os.path.isdir(path):
            return path
    return None

        ['git', 'rev-parse', '--show-toplevel'],
        capture_output=True, text=True, cwd=os.path.dirname(filepath) or '.'
    ).stdout.strip()

[AGENT] I’m checking whether a small local temporal rule with a backend pragma can encode the finite aggregation without adding forbidden top-level axioms.

[CMD] /bin/zsh -lc "cat > /tmp/testptl.tla <<'EOF'
---- MODULE testptl ----
EXTENDS TLAPS, FiniteSets
CONSTANT Q
ASSUME F == IsFiniteSet(Q)
VARIABLE x
THEOREM T == (\\A a \\in Q : <>[](x=a)) => <>[](\\A a \\in Q : x=a)
BY PTL
====
EOF

[AGENT] I’ll run a tiny scratch module to find the exact TLAPS idiom for using `ASSUME/PROVE` theorem instances.

[CMD] /bin/zsh -lc "for variant in 1 2 3 4; do cat > /tmp/testinst.tla <<'EOF'
---- MODULE testinst ----
EXTENDS TLAPS, FiniteSets
THEOREM EAF == ASSUME NEW CONSTANT S, IsFiniteSet(S), NEW TEMPORAL P(_) PROVE (\\A s \\in S : <>[]P(s)) => <>[](\\A s \\in S : P(s))
PROOF OMITTED
CONSTANT Q
ASSUME F == IsFiniteSet(Q)
VARIABLE x
EOF
case "'$variant in
1) cat >> /tmp/testinst.tla <<'"'EOF'
THEOREM T == (\\A a \\in Q : <>[](x=a)) => <>[](\\A a \\in Q : x=a)
<1> DEFINE P(a) == x=a
<1> USE EAF
<1> QED BY F DEF P
====
EOF
;;
2) cat >> /tmp/testinst.tla <<'EOF'
THEOREM T == (\\A a \\in Q : <>[](x=a)) => <>[](\\A a \\in Q : x=a)
<1> DEFINE P(a) == x=a
<1> USE EAF DEF P
<1> QED BY F
====
EOF
;;
3) cat >> /tmp/testinst.tla <<'EOF'
THEOREM T == (\\A a \\in Q : <>[](x=a)) => <>[](\\A a \\in Q : x=a)

<1>1. (ASSUME NEW CONSTANT S, IsFiniteSet(S), NEW TEMPORAL P(_) PROVE (\\A s \\in S : <>[]P(s)) => <>[](\\A s \\in S : P(s)))
  BY EAF
<1> QED BY <1>1, F DEF P
====
EOF
;;
4) cat >> /tmp/testinst.tla <<'EOF'
THEOREM T == (\\A a \\in Q : <>[](x=a)) => <>[](\\A a \\in Q : x=a)
<1> DEFINE P(a) == x=a
<1>1. ASSUME NEW CONSTANT S, IsFiniteSet(S), NEW TEMPORAL R(_)
      PROVE (\\A s \\in S : <>[]R(s)) => <>[](\\A s \\in S : R(s))
  BY EAF
<1> QED BY <1>1, F DEF P
====
EOF
;;
esac
echo --- variant "'$variant ---
~/.tlapm15/bin/tlapm -I ~/.tlapm15/lib/tlaps /tmp/testinst.tla 2>&1 | tail -n 20
done'

[AGENT] I’ll test a direct finite-lattice aggregation proof in scratch, then transplant it if TLAPS accepts it.

[CMD] /bin/zsh -lc "cat > /tmp/testlat.tla <<'EOF'
---- MODULE testlat ----
EXTENDS TLAPS, FiniteSets
ProperSubsetRel(S) == {r \\in (SUBSET S) \\X (SUBSET S) : /\\ r[1] \\subseteq r[2] /\\ r[1] # r[2]}
THEOREM SubsetWellFounded == \\A S : IsFiniteSet(S) => WellFounded(SUBSET S, ProperSubsetRel(S))
PROOF OMITTED
THEOREM LatticeRule == ASSUME NEW S, NEW LT, WellFounded(S, LT), NEW TEMPORAL P(_), NEW TEMPORAL Q
PROVE /\\ Q \\/ (\\E i \\in S : P(i))
      /\\ \\A i \\in S : P(i) ~> (Q \\/ \\E j \\in S : (<<j, i>> \\in LT) /\\ P(j))
      => ((\\E i \\in S : P(i)) ~> Q)
PROOF OMITTED
CONSTANT Q
ASSUME F == IsFiniteSet(Q)
VARIABLE x
THEOREM T == (\\A a \\in Q : <>[](x=a)) => <>[](\\A a \\in Q : x=a)
<1> DEFINE Hyp == \\A s \\in Q : <>[](x=s)
           R(T) == \\A s \\in Q \\ T : [](x=s)
           LT == ProperSubsetRel(Q)
<1>1. Hyp => \\E T \\in SUBSET Q : R(T)
  <2>1. Hyp => R(Q)
    BY DEF R
  <2> QED BY <2>1
<1>2. Hyp => \\A T \\in SUBSET Q :
          R(T) ~> (R({}) \\/ \\E U \\in SUBSET Q : <<U, T>> \\in LT /\\ R(U))
  <2>1. SUFFICES ASSUME NEW T \\in SUBSET Q
                PROVE Hyp => R(T) ~> (R({}) \\/ \\E U \\in SUBSET Q : <<U, T>> \\in LT /\\ R(U))
    OBVIOUS
  <2>2. CASE T # {}
    <3>1. PICK s \\in T : TRUE BY <2>2
    <3>2. s \\in Q BY <2>1, <3>1
    <3> DEFINE U == T \\ {s}
    <3>3. (<<U, T>> \\in LT) /\\ (Q \\ U = (Q \\ T) \\cup {s})
      BY <2>1, <3>1 DEF LT, ProperSubsetRel
    <3>4. Hyp => <>[](x=s)
      BY <3>2 DEF Hyp
    <3>5. R(T) <=> []R(T)
      BY PTL DEF R
    <3>6. <>[](x=s) => [](R(T) => <>(R(T) /\\ [](x=s)))
      BY <3>5, PTL
    <3>7. R(T) /\\ [](x=s) <=> R(U)
      BY <3>3 DEF R
    <3>8. Hyp => (R(T) ~> R(U))
      BY <3>4, <3>6, <3>7, PTL
    <3>9. QED
      BY <3>8, <3>3, PTL
  <2>3. CASE T = {}
    BY PTL
  <2>4. QED BY <2>2, <2>3
<1>3. Hyp => (\\E T \\in SUBSET Q : R(T)) ~> R({})
  BY <1>2, SubsetWellFounded, LatticeRule DEF LT
<1>4. Hyp => <>R({})
  BY <1>1, <1>3, PTL
<1>5. R({}) <=> [](\\A s \\in Q : x=s)
  BY PTL DEF R
<1> QED BY <1>4, <1>5 DEF Hyp
====
EOF
~/.tlapm15/bin/tlapm -I ~/.tlapm15/lib/tlaps /tmp/testlat.tla"

<1>3. QED BY <1>2 DEF P
====
EOF

[AGENT] The clean scratch run revealed the issue: TLAPS drops unlabelled formula assumptions when mixed before a `NEW TEMPORAL`. I’ll reorder those local sequent assumptions so the finite-set hypothesis is preserved.

[CMD] /bin/zsh -lc "cat > /tmp/testinst.tla <<'EOF'
---- MODULE testinst ----
EXTENDS TLAPS, FiniteSets
THEOREM EAF == ASSUME NEW CONSTANT S, IsFiniteSet(S), NEW TEMPORAL P(_) PROVE (\\A s \\in S : <>[]P(s)) => <>[](\\A s \\in S : P(s))
PROOF OMITTED
CONSTANT Q
ASSUME F == IsFiniteSet(Q)
VARIABLE x
THEOREM T == (\\A a \\in Q : <>[](x=a)) => <>[](\\A a \\in Q : x=a)
<1> DEFINE P(a) == x=a
<1>1. ASSUME NEW CONSTANT SS, NEW TEMPORAL PP(_), IsFiniteSet(SS)
      PROVE (\\A ss \\in SS : <>[]PP(ss)) => <>[](\\A ss \\in SS : PP(ss))
  BY EAF
<1>2. (\\A a \\in Q : <>[]P(a)) => <>[](\\A a \\in Q : P(a))
  BY <1>1, F
<1>3. QED BY <1>2 DEF P
====
EOF
rm -rf /tmp/.tlacache .tlacache/testinst.tlaps
~/.tlapm15/bin/tlapm -I ~/.tlapm15/lib/tlaps /tmp/testinst.tla"

    <3>4. Hyp => <>R({{}})
      BY <3>1, <3>3, PTL
    <3>5. R({{}}) <=> []({bs}A s {bs}in Q : Voted(s))
      BY PTL DEF R
    <3>. QED
      BY <3>4, <3>5 DEF Hyp
'''.replace(bs,'\\\\')
s=s[:start]+new2+s[end:]
p.write_text(s)
PY

(***************************************************************************)
(* For liveness, we need to assume that there exists at least one value.   *)
(***************************************************************************)
ASSUME ValueNonempty == Value # {}

(***************************************************************************)
(* TLAPS does not yet reason about ENABLED.  Therefore, we must omit all   *)
(* proofs that involve ENABLED formulas.  To perform as much of the proof  *)
(* as possible, as much as possible we restrict the use of an ENABLED      *)
(* expression to a step asserting that it equals its definition.  ENABLED  *)
(* A is true of a state s iff there is a state t such that the step s -> t *)
(* satisfies A.  It follows from this semantic definition that ENABLED A   *)
(* equals the formula obtained by                                          *)
(*                                                                         *)
(*  1. Expanding all definitions of defined symbols in A until all primes  *)
(*     are priming variables.                                              *)
(*                                                                         *)
(*  2. For each primed variable, replacing every instance of that primed   *)
(*     variable by a new symbol (the same symbol for each primed           *)
(*     variable).                                                          *)
(*

  <2>1. C!ValueNonempty
    BY ValueNonempty
  <2>2. C!LiveSpec <=> C!Spec /'"\\\\ ([]<><<C"'!Next>>_C!vars '"\\\\/ []<>(chosen # {}))

[CMD] /bin/zsh -lc "cat > /tmp/testinst.tla <<'EOF'
---- MODULE testinst ----
EXTENDS TLAPS, FiniteSets
THEOREM EAF == ASSUME NEW CONSTANT S, IsFiniteSet(S), NEW TEMPORAL P(_) PROVE (\\A s \\in S : <>[]P(s)) => <>[](\\A s \\in S : P(s))

====
EOF

[AGENT] Great, the callable form is `Theorem(args...)`. I’ll patch `EventuallyAlwaysForall`/`AlwaysForall`/`C!LiveSpecEquals` calls using that syntax.

[CMD] /bin/zsh -lc "python3 - <<'PY'
from pathlib import Path
p=Path('VoteProof_Liveness.tla')
s=p.read_text()
s=s.replace('''<1>1. C"'!Spec /'"\\\\ []<>(chosen # {}) => C"'!LiveSpec
  <2> USE ValueNonempty, C!ValueNonempty, C!LiveSpecEquals
  <2> QED BY PTL'"''','''<1>1. C"'!Spec /'"\\\\ []<>(chosen # {}) => C"'!LiveSpec
  <2>1. C!LiveSpecEquals
    BY C!LiveSpecEquals(Value, chosen)
  <2>. QED
    BY <2>1, PTL'"''')
s=s.replace('''      BY <1>a, EventuallyAlwaysForall''','''      BY EventuallyAlwaysForall(Q, LAMBDA self : maxBal[self] = b), <1>a''')
s=s.replace('''    BY <1>a, EventuallyAlwaysForall''','''    BY EventuallyAlwaysForall(Q, Voted), <1>a''')
s=s.replace('''      BY AlwaysForall''','''      BY AlwaysForall(Q, LAMBDA self : [\\\\A c \\\\in Ballot : (c > b) => ~ BallotAction(self, c)]_vars)''')
p.write_text(s)
PY

from pathlib import Path
p=Path('VoteProof_Liveness.tla')
s=p.read_text()
s=s.replace('''<1> DEFINE LNext == \\\\E self \\\\in Acceptor, c \\\\in Ballot :
                         /\\\\ BallotAction(self, c)
                         /\\\\ (self \\\\in Q) => (c =< b)''','''<1> DEFINE LNext == \\\\E self \\\\in Acceptor, c \\\\in Ballot :
                         /\\\\ BallotAction(self, c)
                         /\\\\ (self \\\\in Q) => (c =< b)
           High(self) == [\\\\A c \\\\in Ballot : (c > b) => ~ BallotAction(self, c)]_vars''')

           LInv1  == VInv /\\\\ LNInv1''','''<1> DEFINE LNInv1 == \\\\A a \\\\in Q : maxBal[a] =< b
